WiFi is a type of wireless networking technology that allows devices to connect to the internet or communicate with each other over a local area network (LAN). To become an RN, you need to pass the NCLEX-RN exam after completing an associate's or diploma nursing program. A BSN, on the other hand, is a four-year undergraduate degree that prepares you for a career in nursing. While both allow you to work as a registered nurse, having a BSN can provide more job opportunities and higher salary potential.

 RSA encryption is a public-key encryption technology developed by RSA Data Security. The RSA algorithm is based on the difficulty in factoring very large numbers. Based on this principle, the RSA encryption algorithm uses prime factorization as the trap door for encryption. Deducing an RSA key, therefore, takes a huge amount of time and processing power.
